Thanks to leverage, you can buy currency pairs for a multiple of the amount that you invest with CFD. \r\n\r\nThe Forex app consists of the following chapters:\r\n1.\tWhat is Forex?\r\n2.\tAn explanation of Forex rates\r\n3.\tHow do I fulfil a Forex position?\r\n4.\tAn Forex strategy for beginners\r\n5.\tRisk management\r\n6.\tPractical examples\r\n7.\tBrokers: getting started with Forex trade\r\n\r\nAfter you complete the Forex course you know what Forex is and how the currency market works. You can then invest independently in the exchange rate of a currency, use risk management tools and follow a Forex strategy.
